Important News - The Ministry of Education Regularly Holds

Private School Qualification Examinations 147

▲Held in Shanghai, Ping, Yue, and Han on July 1st ｜The regulations for the qualification examinations have been announced｜ The Ministry of Education announced on the 10th thirteen articles of the regulations for the qualification examinations for graduates and former students of unregistered and closed private vocational schools and above, as well as nine articles of the regulations for the committee. The original text is as follows:

▲Regulations for the Qualification Examinations for Graduates and Former Students of Unregistered and Closed Private Vocational Schools and Above

Article 1: Graduates and former students of unregistered and closed private vocational schools and above who possessed one of the following qualifications at the time of admission may apply for the qualification examinations according to the provisions of these regulations: (1) Graduates of senior high schools; (2) Graduates of vocational schools equivalent to the vocational subjects of senior high schools; (3) Graduates of old-system middle schools or those who completed one year of senior high school and entered university preparatory courses for two years; (4) Graduates of old-system middle schools or equivalent schools who have completed two years of service.

Article 2: After registering, applicants must undergo qualification review. Those who do not meet the qualifications will not be allowed to take the examinations.

Article 3: The qualification review will be conducted by the qualification review committee organized by the provincial and municipal education departments at the examination sites.

Article 4: The qualification examinations will be conducted by the qualification examination committee organized by the provincial and municipal education departments at the examination sites. The regulations for the committee will be stipulated separately.

Article 5: The examinations are divided into two parts: basic subjects and specialized subjects. The basic subjects are Party Principles, Chinese Language, Foreign Language, Social Sciences (choose one), and Natural Sciences (choose one). The specialized subjects will be separately stipulated by the examination committee based on the levels of each grade of vocational schools and above. All subjects will be announced seven days before the examination period.

Article 6: The evaluation of applicants' results will be based on the examinations, with reference to qualifications, and assessed separately. If there is service experience, it may also be incorporated and considered appropriately.

Article 7: The results of the qualification examinations will be reported by the examination committee to the Ministry of Education. Graduates with better results may transfer to the last grade of public or registered private vocational schools and above when they recruit students. (This is the result of the qualification examinations. The Ministry of Education will order public and registered private vocational schools and above to be accommodating and not be restricted by Article 4 of the University Regulations and Article 4 of the Revised Vocational School Regulations.) Other graduates and former students will transfer to the corresponding grade according to their level.

Article 8: Applicants whose examination results are too poor and whose academic qualifications are too shallow to transfer to vocational schools and above may transfer to the corresponding grade of senior high school.

Article 9: Applicants will be given a transfer certificate by the Ministry of Education upon completion of the examinations. Its validity is limited to transfer and may not be used to prove other qualifications.

Article 10: When registering, applicants must submit the following documents and fees: (1) Resume, senior high school diploma, vocational school and above diploma or certificate of completion (if there is a service certificate, submit it together); (2) Two recent 4-inch half-length photos; (3) Examination fee of one yuan.

Article 11: The registration date will be determined by the education departments of each province and city, but the deadline is June 20. The registration locations are: Beijing: Beijing Municipal Education Bureau; Shanghai: Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau; Guangzhou: Guangdong Provincial Department of Education; Wuchang: Hubei Provincial Department of Education.

Article 12: The examination locations are divided into four places: Shanghai, Beijing, Guangzhou, and Wuchang. The examination hall will be temporarily determined by the examination committee in each location. The examination date is set to begin on July 1st, and will be held simultaneously in all four places.

Article 13: These regulations will be announced and implemented by the Ministry of Education and will be repealed upon completion of the examinations.

▲Regulations for the Qualification Examination Committee for Graduates and Former Students of Unregistered and Closed Private Vocational Schools and Above

Article 1: This committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Regulations for the Qualification Examinations for Graduates and Former Students of Unregistered and Closed Private Vocational Schools and Above.

Article 2: This committee will have a number of members, who will be appointed or assigned by the provincial and municipal education departments from the following personnel: (1) Current principals and teachers of public or registered private vocational schools and above; (2) Academic experts; (3) Current educational administrative personnel. The number of members in item (3) shall not exceed one-fifth of the total number of members.

Article 3: This committee will have one chairman, who will preside over the affairs of the committee and will be appointed by the director of the provincial or municipal education department from among the members.

Article 4: The examination results of the applicants will be evaluated separately by each member and submitted to the committee for decision.

Article 5: Each subject's examination questions should be secretly drafted by the members of each subject and submitted to the chairman for approval.

Article 6: The evaluation of examination results will be decided by this committee with reference to the scores of each subject and the students' academic qualifications and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and announcement.

Article 7: This committee will have a number of staff members to handle matters such as invigilation and numbering, who will be assigned by the directors of the provincial and municipal education departments from among the staff members of the department.

Article 8: These regulations will be announced and implemented by the Ministry of Education and will be repealed upon completion of the examinations. Announced by the Ministry of Education

Organizational Regulations of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau 148

The Ministry of Education announced on the 10th thirteen articles of the Organizational Regulations of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau. The previously established regulations for the division of labor of the Compilation and Examination Department and the regulations for the Translation Nomenclature Committee will be repealed with immediate effect.

▲Organizational Regulations of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau

Article 1: The Ministry of Education has established the Compilation and Translation Bureau (hereinafter referred to as "the Bureau") to develop culture, promote academics, and review textbooks used in secondary and lower schools.

Article 2: The Bureau will compile, translate, or review various monographs, books, specimens, and instruments in the following categories: 1. Compiling and translating works that clarify culture and advanced academics; 2. Compiling and translating works recognized by world experts as authoritative in academics; 3. Compiling and translating works with extensive content and voluminous volumes that cannot be completed by private individuals in a short period of time; 4. Compiling and translating books necessary for education; 5. Compiling and determining academic translations; 6. Reviewing books, specimens, instruments, and other educational and academic supplies used in secondary and lower schools; 7. Collecting, preserving, and promoting various domestic publications.

Article 3: The Bureau will have one Director, appointed with simplified procedures.

Article 4: The Bureau will have 20 full-time compilers and examiners, 15 compiler and examiner staff members, and a number of specially appointed compilers and examiners, who will be employed by the Director and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 5: The Bureau will have two to four staff members to take charge of matters such as documents, accounting, and general affairs, who will be appointed by the Director and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 6: The Bureau will employ a number of clerks, who will be employed by the Director.

Article 7: The detailed rules of the Bureau's operation and the methods for dividing compilation and examination work will be determined separately.

Article 8: The Bureau will have two meetings for compilation and examination. The detailed rules for their organization will be determined separately.

Article 9: Monographs independently compiled and translated by domestic scholars that meet the provisions of items 1, 2, and 3 of Article 2 and pass the Bureau's review will be given remuneration by the Bureau. Those with significant contributions will be printed by the Bureau, given royalties, and given special bonuses. The rules for printing royalties, remuneration, and bonuses will be determined separately.

Article 10: The methods for submitting textbooks, specimens, and instruments used in secondary and lower schools for review will be handled in accordance with the Textbook Review Regulations and the Textbook Specimen and Instrument Review Regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education.

Article 11: The methods for submitting newly published books in the country will be handled in accordance with the New Book Submission Regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education.

Article 13: At the end of each fiscal year, the Compilation and Translation Bureau should prepare a report on the overall situation of the work for the whole year and the work plan for the next year and submit it to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 13: These regulations will be submitted by the Ministry of Education to the Executive Yuan for approval and then promulgated and implemented by ministerial order. This City

The Municipal Education Bureau Plans to Establish a Zoo 151

In the area south of Shanghai in this city, there are very few public parks for citizens to visit and relax during their leisure time. The Municipal Education Bureau is aware of this and has actively designed a plan. In addition to arranging the Confucius Temple into a park and preparing to open a public education center, it also plans to establish a zoo at the original site of Qinpu near Panfang in Penglai Road. It previously submitted a plan and was approved by the municipal government to allocate funds for construction. However, the site was occupied by the 28th Wireless Telegraph Station of the Ministry of Military Affairs, and it was temporarily unable to be realized. Now, the Municipal Education Bureau has sent personnel to negotiate its recovery and has jointly reorganized and constructed the site with the Public Works Bureau. In addition, some of the tigers, leopards, lions, elephants, and other rare birds and animals to be displayed in the park have already been purchased, and various others are being procured. People from all walks of life who are willing to donate various birds and animals are welcome. The Citizens' Education Center

Plans to Open Part of the Garden Landscape 152

The construction of the internal buildings and the arrangement of the garden landscape of the Municipal Public Education Center, which is planned to be established in the Confucius Temple in the west of this city, has been mostly completed. The model specimens and other exhibits have also been purchased and prepared in order. It was expected to be completed and opened soon. However, due to the war, the work in the center was suspended. Now that the war has come to an end and local order is gradually returning to normal, the unfinished projects and all ongoing matters have been jointly planned and actively handled by the Education and Public Works Bureaus. It is planned to open all or part of the garden landscape first to satisfy the public's desire. Physical Education

All Schools to Emphasize Physical Education 154

▲Strictly Prohibit Male Students from Wearing Long Robes with Narrow Sleeves and Female Students from Wearing Cheongsams That Reach the Ankles

Nanjing, November 11 (This Newspaper) He Yingqin telegraphed President Wang and Minister of Education Zhu, requesting that the Ministry of Education formulate a detailed plan to supervise and direct all schools across the country to emphasize physical education, promote martial arts, and strictly prohibit male students from wearing long robes with narrow sleeves and female students from wearing cheongsams that reach the ankles. Chinese Tennis Association

Begins to Solicit Registrations 155

▲The Court Repair is Completed and Play Will Begin Immediately ▲The First Committee Meeting Tomorrow

During the Japanese invasion of China, our people suffered greatly, and various sports competitions in Shanghai have been suspended for more than three months. Now that the Shanghai side has signed a ceasefire agreement, although the national crisis has not yet ended, we must not give up eating because of choking. This is precisely the time for us to strengthen our bodies and serve the country. The weather is gradually getting warmer, and soccer and basketball are no longer suitable. However, tennis is the only beautiful outdoor sport in the summer. The Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association has already held a meeting to prepare, and the league will begin around mid-June. It is now learned that the repair of the Chinese Tennis Association's court has been completed and play will begin immediately. The association hopes that all former members will enthusiastically register and join as in previous years to prepare for selecting a team to participate in the Western League competition to maintain the reputation of the Chinese who have dominated for several years. The association has appointed Hu Jiansheng, Hu Yunlai, Li Baojun, Ouyang Xuchu, and Ling Xitao as committee members to preside over the association's administration. The first meeting will be held tomorrow (the 13th) at 12:30 at Dun Tuomo to discuss the association's constitution and other matters.

The Difficulties in Developing Foreign Funds 161

During March and April of this year, after the 19th Route Army retreated from Shanghai, the current silver dollars in various ports along the Yangtze River and inland were successively transferred to Shanghai. Almost all the essence of the five southern provinces was concentrated in Shanghai. However, the sudden acquisition of a large amount of cash by silver and money dealers, coupled with the unrest in the current situation, has made it impossible for the funds to flow smoothly. This situation of continuous inflow without outflow, with daily buying and selling within the market, cannot inject huge amounts of funds into society. As far as recent observations are concerned, the arrival of funds from other sources in Shanghai has not stopped. It can be expected that if no efforts are made to develop smooth flow, the premium price trend will eventually decline. However, at present, cocoons are generally on the market. Due to poor harvests, there are fears that there will be a large demand. Therefore, the hope of resolving the difficult situation for the time being is slim. Certificates

She County Green Tea Has Been Weighed 167

Since the beginning of summer, She County green tea has been completely picked by the famous mountain households. The foreign firm store has opened the weighing, and the opening price for Nanlu goods is 95 yuan, and the opening price for Xilu goods is from 68 yuan to 76 yuan. Later, due to the rush of shop customers from various shops, the market price soared by six or seven yuan. In addition, due to excessive frost and dew last winter, the output of each mountain head was reduced, and there is a tendency for the market price to continue to rise.

Xing'an Tea Production Declines 168

The tea production in Xing'an, Ganzhou, has always been rich, especially the production of famous mountains is the most superior. In previous years, the Honglu tea brands of the Yangzhuang River Port and the Hanzhou shop used to send people here to purchase. After the decline of the River Port tea market, the route of Xing tea has become narrower, only holding a small number of sales fields in the shop, and the market price has also decreased day by day. The mountain households believe that tea cannot be relied upon, so they do not add cultivation, and the output is also decreasing year by year. In the past two years, Ge Yuan, where tea is produced, has been occupied by red bandits, and there is no production. Although the Communist bandits in the area have been wiped out by the national army this year, it is still difficult to eradicate the remaining shares. At the moment, farmers are giving priority to their urgent plans, and they are mostly busy with rice farming, and do not pay much attention to tea. There is still no tea market to speak of.

Fuliang Green Tea Is Being Picked 169

Fuliang tea is divided into red and green. The green tea in the Cangjiawan Shijing area bordering Wubei is quite good in terms of water leaf quality and taste. This year, because the foreign Hongzhuang tea brands in Fuliang have been greatly reduced compared to the old days, and other places are far away and inconvenient for transportation, the Qing tea is still produced as usual. Recently, the sky suddenly cleared and rained suddenly, and the tea buds are developing faster and faster. The mountain households think that the amount of tea needed by the tea houses in Xiutun will inevitably increase, so they pick the tender heads early in order to increase the selling price. Since the day before yesterday (2nd), they have been picking them one after another. However, the tea trees in the fields that are exposed to the wind have not developed very well due to the freezing of the cold snow last winter. The output is not expected to be a good harvest.

Jinhua Spring Cocoons Have Already Seen New 170

▲Insufficient silk spitting due to cold weather… The cocoon body is not good ▲

▲The cocoon market has not yet opened.▲

The silkworm flood season in Jinhua Prefecture is earlier than in Hangzhou and Shaoxing. This year, due to the severe weather, the native species cultivated by farmers were completely discarded. Only the foreign species of silkworms still have a surplus. However, after they went on the cluster, the climate was cold and the silkworms did not spit enough silk. The new cocoons have now been off the cluster, but the cocoon body is not good. The cocoon market has not yet been leased out, and has not yet been opened. There is no market for new cocoons. Farmers are generally prepared to bake them themselves using native stoves.

The Powder Market Continues to Weaken 174

▲A Glimpse of the Current Market▲

We oppose dictatorship, and we also do not acknowledge double leadership! These are the two most incisive sentences that Mr. Sun Zhesheng said on behalf of our people. Looking around the country, it is fragmented, the landscape has changed color, and it has been reduced to a broken-down situation with a myriad of problems, which everyone unanimously says is the result of five years of dictatorial politics. Returning from Southeast Asia 181

— Zou Mengchan

My cousin, Ms. Chen Yiyu, and Ms. Wu Ruiying, the wife of national language expert Guo Houjue, have been teaching at the Ipoh Girls' School in Perak, Southeast Asia for many years. This time, hearing that the national crisis is pressing and angered by the Japanese army's brutality and the bitter fighting of our 19th Route Army, they care about their homeland and, motivated by righteous indignation, they wished to participate in the rear-area nursing work. So they resolutely resigned from their teaching positions and came to Shanghai together. Recently, the field hospital has ended its service, and it is a pity that they did not get to participate. Although their wishes were not fulfilled, their sincerity is commendable. Yesterday, I received an invitation by telephone and was able to chat with them for several days. What they described about the local customs and scenery in Southeast Asia can provide material for discussion. So I recorded a few things as follows. The enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese for patriotism Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia seem to have no national protection and are subject to unequal treaties. Their position is different from that of the expatriates of powerful countries. Therefore, they all hope that the nation will prosper and be protected. Hearing that the former 19th Route Army fought bloody battles against the Japanese and repeatedly performed meritorious deeds, they were all delighted and actively contributed. Although the Perak port donated the least, the amount still reached 40,000. From this, we can see a glimpse of the enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese for patriotism. The importance of the national language Most of the overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia are from southern China. In addition to the dialects of various places, there is no standard language. Therefore, the education sector especially promotes the national language. Now, even elementary school students who are eight or nine years old can speak very pure national language. As for school teachers, their proficiency in the national language is particularly important for their advancement. Simplicity of life Southeast Asia is located in the tropics, so the climate is like early summer in China all year round. Within a day, the morning is like spring, and the temperature at noon is usually between 77 and 80 degrees Fahrenheit. The highest record is only 96 degrees. Therefore, men's and women's clothing is also simplified accordingly. Women wear white shirts and blue skirts, and men have only one or two sets of summer suits, which are enough for the whole year. Southeast Asia produces abundant rice, and vegetables, fish, and meat are especially cheap. Life is simple, so it is very easy to make a living.

Anecdotes of Resisting the Enemy: The Iron Buddha 182

When the Shanghai Incident first broke out, the enemy army used Park as its headquarters. One day, our army sent forty men divided into ten teams to attack. First, four men tested the waters, and the rest were scattered to the left and right. The Japanese chieftain saw four men intruding into the park gate from afar and laughed loudly, ordering them to be captured alive to carry out his brutal torture. So they went out in all directions to encircle and pursue them. Our army quickly retreated like flying, unable to be caught. When they returned, all the cannons in the park were firing in unison, and the enemy flags had been removed and replaced with our national emblem. They were greatly shocked and fled in all directions. At that time, our main force had already covered the area, and none of them escaped. In this battle, we captured their entire force.

A certain soldier, Mr. So-and-so, had his femur bone hit by a bullet and needed surgery. The doctor said that anesthesia should be used. Mr. So-and-so refused, saying, "I am not afraid of risking my life, let alone a small cut." He calmly underwent the surgery without any fear. Soon, fresh blood gushed out, and he gritted his teeth and shouted, "Kill all the remnants of the Japanese army." Before he finished speaking, the bullet suddenly jumped out from the bone. Mr. So-and-so's wife heard this and praised his loyalty and courage, rushing to comfort him and covering him with a silk quilt. Everyone who heard about it was moved.

Our army's Cantonese pilots have many divine skills. The enemy fears them like tigers. One day, during an engagement, the enemy dropped bombs from a large aircraft. Our aircraft saw it and pursued it, climbing above it and pressing down hard. The enemy aircraft could not escape and was forced to land on the ground and captured.

One day, an enemy aircraft dropped a bomb. As soon as it was released, our army's aircraft shot it down. It happened to collide with the bomb, and the aircraft was destroyed. It was as if heaven was intervening, not human power.

Old Peking 183

— Mei Ying

Recently, the Central and Star cinemas in Shanghai are screening a good domestic sound film called "Old Peking." This title caught my eye and couldn't help but evoke emotions. Peking, referred to as "Old Peking," is of course different from the Peking of today. However, the Peking of today, the place where dragons coiled and tigers crouched, has, since the Shanghai Incident suddenly occurred and the national capital was moved to Luoyang, also ceased to be the Peking of today. Recently, the Sino-Japanese agreement has been signed, and the government officials can return in peace and leisurely recount their intimate feelings in the Qin Huai district and maintain the solemnity of the capital in the stone city. Otherwise, if the Japanese army continues to press on relentlessly, in order to resist for the long term, we will inevitably have to continue to move west from Luoyang's temporary capital, to Xi'an's secondary capital and eventually to the peaks of the Himalayas. If this unfortunately happens, then the so-called Peking of today will inevitably also be named Old Peking. Alas.

Can you write a letter to her in my presence according to what I said?" An Yutian frowned and answered, "I'll just have to do as you say. Are you going to write that letter now?" Liang Xiaoyun smiled, "You can write it tomorrow morning. But don't frown and look forced, lest you regret it later. You should turn me down right now if you can't do it." An Yutian quickly reached out to cover her cherry lips and said, "Okay. Don't say it. If you still don't believe me, I can get out of bed and swear to heaven." Liang Xiaoyun held him down gently and said, "It's not that I don't believe you. It's just that I still have an even harder problem that I haven't finished talking about. You're already frowning, how can I feel at ease? But I definitely don't want you to swear. I only require that you write the letter tomorrow morning and then go to your apartment together. Immediately move all your luggage to my place. Just leave the letter to the doorman to give to Li Wenxia. From then on, we'll be living together. All actions can no longer be hidden from me. That's a stronger guarantee than anything else. It's not that I'm too petty. It's just that to leash this wild horse of yours, I have to do this. Are you in or not? You have to give me a clear answer."

Difficult to Have, Difficult to Lack 185

— Buddha

Since the January 28th Incident, land transportation between Shanghai and Suzhou has been completely cut off, and only water transportation remains. Therefore, in the past two months, there have been more than 30 major cases of ship robbery, which is truly appalling. Among the 30-odd robbery cases, the most noteworthy should be the previous robbery of the Sun and Yang families in Wuxi, involving about 500,000 to 600,000 yuan, and the recent major losses suffered by a wealthy man from Suzhou who was moving back to Suzhou, amounting to about 400,000 yuan. In addition, smaller losses are naturally countless. This is originally a lucky occurrence for the bandits and a gift from the Japanese cavalry. What else can be said? However, in the face of merciless artillery fire, constant tremors, and iron birds dropping bombs all over the sky, it is truly a hardship for ordinary people. If they don't flee, they will either be buried in the flames or suffer the tragic consequences of rape and plunder. They have no choice but to flee. But for those who flee, there are two kinds of people who are very miserable. If they go to the concession to rent a house, they have no money. If they stay in a hotel, they have even less money. There is no way out, they can only carry their bedding and bring their broken, essential items to several refugee shelters, where they are given a few bowls of thin porridge and a few dried radish strips, which are the most vitamin C-rich health foods. Dozens of families are crammed into a large room, for them to enjoy. The air in this room is naturally extremely tense. Some are sick, some are dazed, some cannot walk, some are crying, some are laughing, and some are in a state of despair. Such a chaotic clamor and state of confusion is naturally impossible to organize under special circumstances. In addition, there are several young Boy Scouts guarding the door for you. From the outside, it looks like a grand scale. This is the suffering of those who have no money. Do they call for a few large boats? No, they are afraid of danger on the road. Do they take a steamer? No, they are afraid that a few "bandit brothers" will come to ask for a consultation. But there is no other way. However, steamers seem to be safer than civilian boats. Even those who are usually unwilling to compromise have no choice but to send their family's life and property, more or less, onto the steamer as much as possible. Unexpectedly, there is a gunshot. That's bad! By then it will be too late. If they had known this would happen, why did they act as they did in the first place? Fortunately, the danger on the steamer passed safely, but robbery cases in the concession also occur from time to time. If, in the evening, five or six friends suddenly come in through the back door, wielding pistols and warning them not to make a sound, then they have no choice but to obey and cannot resist. This is the suffering of those who have money. Money is omnipotent, which is the most fashionable and effective slogan in modern times. But now that the country is in such a state, and society is in such a state, I can only advise a few wealthy gentlemen not to be so calculating and only focus on profits. (It is convenient to be convenient.) To be honest, living in a chaotic society, the more wealth you have, the more worries you have. Naturally, you cannot live without wealth, but if you have too much wealth, it is the burden of wealth, not the blessing of wealth. Recently, such huge robbery cases have occurred repeatedly on the Suzhou-Shanghai road, and I feel even more that hoarding wealth invites robbery and that ivory tusks invite destruction. The power of money is not omnipotent, but truly evil. The cleverest ones are naturally those old gentlemen. They immediately send the money that they usually desperately squeeze from the common people to foreign banks. Seeing that the situation is not right, they use an excuse of inspection, travel, or study, and slip away to become expatriates in foreign countries. This is such an easy and perceptive thing. Alas!

Science

Artificial Silk 186

— Qu Yin

China has always been the world's supplier of silk fabrics. Recently, because China is unwilling to improve its silk and tea, it is on the verge of a sharp decline. At the same time, the import of foreign artificial silk is increasing day by day. Most of the silk stockings, silk shirts, silk scarves, and other popular items on the market are artificial silk fabrics. I am afraid that many Chinese people do not know what artificial silk is. I will introduce its source here. Natural silk is a protein. It has an odor when burned and leaves carbon residue. Artificial silk is made from cellulose made from wood. It has a flame when burned and no odor, and it does not leave carbon residue. It has a greater luster than natural silk, but it is not as strong or durable. There are four manufacturing methods:

(1) Slowly mix 400 parts of crude nitric acid with a specific gravity of 1.42 and 1000 parts of concentrated sulfuric acid with a specific gravity of 1.833. When cooled to 20 degrees Celsius, add 55 parts of bleached cellulose or cotton that has already been made. Soak it for 24 hours between 15 and 20 degrees, take it out, drain it, wash it with clean water, and dry it in a 25-degree atmosphere to form nitrated cellulose. Then dissolve the nitrated cellulose in a mixture of 40 parts of anhydrous alcohol and 60 parts of ether-removed ether (if it does not dissolve, it is because it has been soaked in nitric sulfuric acid for too long, or the nitric sulfuric acid is too concentrated, and it has become trinitrocellulose. Cotton gunpowder is because the nitric sulfuric acid is too dilute, and the soaking time is too short, and it only becomes mononitrocellulose). Place this solution in a can with countless small needle-tip holes. Apply pressure from above, and the cellulose solution will become thread-like and ejected from below. At the same time, allow the solvent contained within to evaporate on its own in a flowing high-temperature air, or directly inject it into water so that the alcohol is absorbed into water. The cellulose then becomes silk, but this silk still contains two nitro groups NO2. If they are not removed, it is most likely to catch fire or burn. It must then be reduced with an acidic sodium sulfide solution NaSH or an acidic ammonium sulfide solution NH4SH to remove the two NO2, so there is no risk of silk stockings exploding on the dance floor.

(2) Add alkali to a copper sulfate CuSO4 solution in Schweizer's Solution to produce copper dihydroxide Cu(OH)2. Temporarily dissolve this in concentrated ammonia solution to form a blue liquid of Cu(NH3)4(OH)2. This liquid can dissolve cellulose. Use this liquid containing cellulose, and like the method above, press it through small holes into dilute sulfuric acid. The cellulose is restored to silk.

(3) Dissolve cellulose in a mixture of carbon disulfide CS2 and caustic soda. Pass this dissolved cellulose solution through the same chemical process as in the second method. The chemical formula of the transformation is as follows: (C6H10O5)X + XCS2 + XNaOH = (C6H9O5CS2Na)X + XH2O

(4) Mix Essigsaureanhydrid (CH3CO)2O with a small amount of sulfuric acid, soak cellulose in it for ten hours, take it out, and dissolve it in chloroform. Then, like the first method, press it into water to form the final product. This is the most recently invented method, and the product produced is the best of all artificial silks.

A Sketch of Dandy Students 187

— Ben Xi

As soon as the class bell rang, it was followed by a burst of loud footsteps and movements, like birds rejoicing after being confined in a cage for a long time, filling S School. So, those romantic students, generally known as dandies, heard the class bell and called it a frantic cry of liberation and a life-saving bell.

"Tomorrow is the fifth of September. It's a holiday prescribed by the Ministry of Education. It probably won't be an exception this year, right? Look, the peace agreement has already been signed, and Shanghai is still a prosperous Shanghai. We should go out and have some fun! Ha! Moon, are you going tonight?" The one who said these words was C, nicknamed "Wealthy Son." At this time, he had already sat lively on a long rectangular table.

"That's right!" E said. "It's so boring!" E was already feeling bored due to the weariness of class. Hearing this proposal, the party members of the same faction would never object, so it quickly passed by a show of hands.

"Why hasn't the holiday notice been posted on the announcement board yet?" E asked hesitantly. C said, "Go ask the general affairs office."

"This year, the studies sacrificed for the Shanghai war, even if we try desperately to make up for them, are still not enough. No more holidays at all in the future."

They were twenty minutes disappointed when they heard this. They deeply hated that Shanghai had to fight a war, so that they couldn't even have holidays. But a new consciousness immediately took over. They instinctively felt that they had already had enough fun during the war. So, they silently went to the classroom to attend the last class of the day.

"Wealthy Son" was finally unable to contain his boredom and said angrily to E, "Tonight, no matter what, let's go to Moon and have a great time to vent our anger!" E silently agreed.

In Moon, which emitted a ghostly glow like phosphorus, "Wealthy Son" and E were embracing trembling, living flesh. The song strings of the music were pulling out intoxicating dreams. They were immersed in it, they were delighted, and of course, whether they would happily go to class tomorrow was another matter.

After Dinner 188

— Wu

After dinner, everyone's faces showed satisfied expressions. Mr. Jiang was picking his teeth, and Mr. Yi, wearing a suit, was holding a cup of tea. They were both lying on the sofa in silence, quietly. Soon, Mrs. Cheng came down from upstairs, carrying her fourth child in her arms. She said;

It Is Their Fault 191

— Ling Fen

Yesterday, I overheard a conversation between two miserly rent collectors, Mr. H and Mr. S?

A: (How have things been in your area recently? Is the rent being collected regularly?)

B: (Oh, don't even mention it. Although our properties aren't in the war zone, out of the thirty-odd houses we have, over twenty haven't paid rent for four months. When we talk to them, they just claim to be short on cash, or say there are rent-free arrangements being offered elsewhere, and they'll decide later... I don't know how things are on your end?)

A: (It's the same here! Can you think of any solutions?)

B: (Yeah, I guess we're just unlucky.)

A: (That's for sure! But there's worse... I heard that they've already decided to waive rent for the first three months, and reduce rent by × percent from the fourth to the sixteenth month.)

B: (That's terrible! With that, we've already lost the interest, and now they want to waive rent and reduce it by × percent. Won't our commissions also decrease?)

A: (It's the same for me! In any case, the most hateful thing is the ×× army. We wanted them to resist,...)

B: (Yes, otherwise the war might not have happened, and we wouldn't have been affected by rent waivers and reductions!)

A: (Yes, and the ×× army's resistance isn't naturally beneficial to us, and it might not even be beneficial to ××!)

B: (Oh...)

Movie

The Total Love of the President 192

"The Total Love of the President" is the latest major silent film. The three main actors are Ivan Mosjoukine, famous for "The White Devil," Miss Suzy, famous for "The Extravagant Life of an Actress," and Mingo, the number one dog star of the time. Having just one of these three stars would be enough to draw crowds, and now with all three, the results are better than anyone expected. Moreover, the plot is noble, implying that one must strive to succeed in life. It offers unique insights on male-female issues, and is especially thought-provoking. Ivan Mosjoukine's artistry has long been praised. He delivers a very strong performance from beginning to end, and the intelligent dog Mingo follows him closely. His comedic moments are hilarious, and his cleverness is astonishing. People sigh that they have never seen anything like it before. This film premiered at the Paris Cinema on Avenue Joffre yesterday, and viewers are full of praise.

The Mysterious and Bizarre (The Poison Arrow Mystery) 193

It was probably about two years ago that a shocking poison arrow case was discovered in a British region, causing quite a stir. Anyone would think that the killer must be a red-haired, green-eyed robber who doesn't bat an eye at murder. But the result was beyond the detectives' expectations; the culprit was actually a beautiful woman. As for the twists and turns of the case and why the beauty committed this illegal act, there isn't time to explain it all now. I heard that the Carlton is showing "The House of the Snow" (The Poison Arrow Mystery). The plot of this film is based on this case, and the male and female actors starring in this film are all famous stars of the silver screen, able to fully bring out the spirit of the case. This is indeed a rare and realistic detective film to see.

The Ethically Bizarre Masterpiece (Iron Evidence) 194

The ethical masterpiece "The Silent Witness" (Iron Evidence), which opens tomorrow at the Nanjing Grand Theatre, is a Fox Film Corporation production based on a world-famous play. The main actor, Rainer Adde-Höhde, is a famous stage star who has starred in the play on Broadway more than two hundred times. His inner and facial expressions are unique, shocking the world of the arts. Greta Nissen, who plays the prostitute, is the star of the sensational "Passion in the Desert." Her passionate performance is extremely intoxicating, making this film the crown jewel of passionate films. The film vividly portrays the love of a father for his son, using a bizarre and unpredictable murder case as the backdrop. The film tells the story of a young man's affair with a prostitute. The woman behaves improperly, and the young man strangles her, but uses too much force, and the woman dies. The young man, frightened and panicked, confesses to his parents. During the confrontation in court, the father tries his best to protect his son, but the ironclad evidence is all there, and even a hundred mouths cannot argue it away. The case is settled, but the one who killed the woman is definitely not the young man. In the end, the truth comes out, and the plot is twisted, bizarre, and unusual.

The Variety of Shows at the Cathay 195

The Cathay Grand Theatre on Avenue Joffre is opening today with the endlessly hilarious comedy "Bean Hunks" (Old Soldiers), starring the comedic duo Laurel and Hardy. The two men's artistic talent is already well-known and needs no introduction. Their previous film, "Pardon Us," which opened in Shanghai, was especially popular. The highlights of "Bean Hunks" are even richer than those of "Pardon Us." Moreover, it is heard that in order to please the audience, the Cathay is also specially adding: (1) A documentary of the Olympic Games, (2) A colorful song and dance film, and (3) "Dog Brothers," a hilarious film starring a full cast of dog stars. Such a program can be said to be all-encompassing, with everything that one could want, and is truly worth seeing.

Notice Board

The Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court 196

▲One criminal judgment concerns Huang Quanlin's appeal against the first instance judgment of the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District District Court in the case of robbery. The court's judgment is as follows: (Main text) The original judgment is revoked. Huang Quanlin, a recidivist, is sentenced to fourteen years of imprisonment for jointly robbing with more than three people while carrying weapons. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be counted as one day of imprisonment for every two days. The two pistols and twelve bullets are confiscated. ▲One civil judgment concerns Hu Zhetin's appeal against the lawsuit with the French company, Michelman, for payment of goods. The court's judgment is as follows: (Main text) The original is returned to the appellee, and the appellee is paid the amount of goods, silver seven thousand one hundred and eighty-five taels, four mace, and nine candareens. Furthermore, from June 20, 1931, until the date of final execution, interest on the amount of the goods shall be paid at an annual rate of five percent for late payment. The appellant's remaining appeal and the appellee's remaining claims in the first instance are both rejected. The costs of litigation in the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellant four-fifths and the appellee one-fifth (May 10th)

The movable property in the house has been seized by the court and is about to be auctioned. The location and number of the lane mentioned may be incorrect, and the original text of the respondent Liu Zuojun's transliteration must also be stated in detail for verification.
